diplomacy = {
	
	#Roman allies / socii in Italia
	dependency = { first = ROM second = MSP subject_type = socius_subject }	#Messapia
	dependency = { first = ROM second = BRT subject_type = socius_subject }	#Bruttia
	dependency = { first = ROM second = LCA subject_type = socius_subject }	#Lucania
	dependency = { first = ROM second = APU subject_type = socius_subject }	#Apulia
	dependency = { first = ROM second = FRE subject_type = socius_subject }	#Frentania
	dependency = { first = ROM second = PEL subject_type = socius_subject }	#Pelignia
	dependency = { first = ROM second = UMB subject_type = socius_subject }	#Umbria
	dependency = { first = ROM second = MRS subject_type = socius_subject }	#Marsia
	dependency = { first = ROM second = ANO subject_type = socius_subject }	#Ancona
	dependency = { first = ROM second = HCL subject_type = socius_subject }	#Heraclea
	dependency = { first = ROM second = NUC subject_type = socius_subject }	#Nuceria
	dependency = { first = ROM second = LOC subject_type = socius_subject }	#Locri
	dependency = { first = ROM second = RHG subject_type = socius_subject }	#Rhegium
	dependency = { first = ROM second = PEN subject_type = socius_subject }	#Pentria
	dependency = { first = ROM second = CAD subject_type = socius_subject }	#Caudinia
	dependency = { first = ROM second = HRP subject_type = socius_subject }	#Hirpinia
	dependency = { first = ROM second = VLT subject_type = socius_subject }	#Volaterria
	dependency = { first = ROM second = VTL subject_type = socius_subject }	#Vetulonia
	dependency = { first = ROM second = ARI subject_type = socius_subject }	#Arretia
	dependency = { first = ROM second = CLS subject_type = socius_subject }	#Clusia
	dependency = { first = ROM second = PIE subject_type = socius_subject }	#Picentia
	
	#Roman subjects outside of Italia
	dependency = { first = ROM second = AET subject_type = client_state }	#Aetolian League, had to fight in the same wars as the Romans
	dependency = { first = ROM second = AKR subject_type = tributary }	#Akarnania
	dependency = { first = ROM second = AMK subject_type = tributary }	#Ambracia, declared a Free City of Rome
	dependency = { first = ROM second = RHO subject_type = tributary }	#Rhodes, ally that lost autonomy to Rome
	dependency = { first = ROM second = LYC subject_type = tributary }	#Lycia, given autonomy from Rhodes by Rome
	dependency = { first = ROM second = CIA subject_type = tributary }	#Caria, given autonomy from Rhodes by Rome
	dependency = { first = ROM second = GAD subject_type = feudatory }	#Gadir, Punic city in Iberia
	
	#Roman tribal vassals
	dependency = { first = ROM second = VNT subject_type = foederati_subject }	#Veneto, foederati subject, close ally of Rome since Second Punic War
	dependency = { first = ROM second = INS subject_type = vassal_tribe }	#Insubria, autonomous ally in cisalphine
	dependency = { first = ROM second = CNM subject_type = vassal_tribe }	#Cenomannia, autonomous ally in cisalphine
	dependency = { first = ROM second = TAU subject_type = vassal_tribe }	#Taurinia, autonomous ally in cisalphine
	
	#Illyrian vassals of Rome
	dependency = { first = ROM second = DRI subject_type = vassal_tribe }	#Daorsia
	dependency = { first = ROM second = ABI subject_type = vassal_tribe }	#Ardiaei, remnant king in Rhizon
	dependency = { first = ROM second = LBA subject_type = vassal_tribe }	#Labeatia, subjugated after defeat of Gentius
	dependency = { first = ROM second = LBN subject_type = vassal_tribe }	#Libernia, submitted to Rome
	dependency = { first = ROM second = DIT subject_type = vassal_tribe }	#Iapodia, submitted to Rome

	#Rome Macedonian Client States / Client Republics
	dependency = { first = ROM second = MAC subject_type = tributary }	#Pella
	dependency = { first = ROM second = TSK subject_type = tributary }	#Thessalonike
	dependency = { first = ROM second = APH subject_type = tributary }	#Amphipolis
	dependency = { first = ROM second = PLG subject_type = tributary }	#Pelagonia
	
	#Roman-Jewish treaty
	guarantee = { first = ROM second = JUD }	#Judea
	
	#Independent allies of Rome
	guarantee = { first = ROM second = MAS }	#Massalia/Massilia, autonomous ally of Rome
	guarantee = { first = ROM second = EPO }	#Emporion, autonomous ally of Rome
	guarantee = { first = ROM second = CYR }	#Ptolemy Physcon in Cyrenaica, supported by Rome
